S2·S3 |↑↓↑⟩: particles 2 and 3 are |↓↑⟩, so (-3/8 ) ħ².

S2·S3 |↓↑↑⟩: (1/4 ) ħ².

Thus, the eigenvalues of H are related to the eigenvalues of S².

For three spin-1/2 particles, the possible total spins are S=3/2 and S=1/2.
